    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',

But a price on her head – wanted: dead or half-alive – means her survival depends on teaming up with Bones. And no matter how hard Cat tries to keep things professional between them, she’ll find that desire lasts forever … and Bones won’t let her get away again.</span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/117882103?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">People who I want to confuse</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer117882103" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3435145355516204727">You know how sometimes I choose to litter my reviews with innapropriate words or themes? Like Austin Powers taking a giant shit in my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/90063181' rel='nofollow noopener'>Guilty Pleasures review</a>, or my reoccuring use of the word 'balls' in my <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/109952719' rel='nofollow noopener'>Shiver Review</a>?<br/><br/>Well, the theme and word for the day is buttsecks.<br/><br/>As in: <i>I was innocently reading One Foot in the Grave by Jeaniene Frost when the two main characters suddenly had buttsecks.</i><br/><br/>Now, I'm a shameless, wanton hussy with super magical slut powers, just like any other girl, but some thin</span>
  <span id="freeText3435145355516204727" style="display:none">You know how sometimes I choose to litter my reviews with innapropriate words or themes? Like Austin Powers taking a giant shit in my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/90063181" rel="nofollow noopener">Guilty Pleasures review</a>, or my reoccuring use of the word 'balls' in my <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/109952719" rel="nofollow noopener">Shiver Review</a>?<br /><br />Well, the theme and word for the day is buttsecks.<br /><br />As in: <i>I was innocently reading One Foot in the Grave by Jeaniene Frost when the two main characters suddenly had buttsecks.</i><br /><br />Now, I'm a shameless, wanton hussy with super magical slut powers, just like any other girl, but some things just kind of throw me off. Like buttsecks.<br /><br />Buttsecks.<br /><br />Yes, I'm not spelling it right on purpose.<br /><br />Cat has been working in her secret organization for four years and hasn't seen Bones since she dumped him when she suddenly finds herself the target of a bounty and...Well, I don't care about the rest because there's buttsecks!<br /><br />Like the first book, One Foot in the Grave contains a lot of sex, action, supernatural dudes and only moderate-to-light buttsecks.<br /><br />Buttsecks.<br /><br />The storyline is quite good with a clever little ending which contains absolutely no buttsecks at all.<br /><br />The whole story is a bit of a blur. Tatiana tipped me off to the fact that there could possibly be buttsecks present. Interested, and ever increasingly perverted, I decided to see how the author would pull it off and what the author would describe it like. So basically, for me, this story started out with a beginning that was lacking in buttsecks, buttsecks, and the end of the story that was buttsecks-free.<br /><br />Now I'm wondering why the author decided to do this. Was it to be different? To recreate a norm? To show this as a normal part of couple's love lives that is often not spoken about?<br /><br />If it's the first then it almost certainly worked for me. I've already used buttsecks thirteen times in this review and I'm almost certainly going to use it more (buttsecks!)<br /><br />If she's creating a norm in fiction, or to show a little seen side of secks acts that aren't talked about in polite society, then I can't, as a reader, relate but I can appreciate her for her efforts. <br /><br />It was certainly different... I can't say that I found it a huge turn on to read about, but luckily Frost threw in several other moments to kind of even it all off.<br /><br />So, in closing... buttsecks.<br /><br />That's all I have to say, folks.<br /><br />Buttsecks.<br /> <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3435145355516204727" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

So you tried to get on with your life because you believed it would never work between us. But you see, I couldn't get on with my life because I knew we could work. So you tried to get on with your life because you believed it would never work between us. But you see, I couldn't get on with my life because I knew we could work. I've been looking for you every day since you left me, Kitten, and I'm sick of being without you. You've had your shot at things, now let me have mine."-Bones</b><br><br>Yay Bones and Cat are back in, One Foot in the Grave, the 2nd book in the Night Huntress series. And they are just as awesome and kick ass as they are in the first book. This book picks up right where the last book leaves off. At the end of the last book, Halfway to the Grave , Cat leaves Bones to protect him , and her mom. She goes to work for Homeland Security Paranomarl dept. This book starts 4 years later. Cat does her job, hangs out with her friend Denise, and trains her team, but she isn't happy. She misses Bones and still loves him. when she runs into Bones again at her friend Denise's wedding all those feeling that she tried to bury come rushing to the surface. When Bones tells her that he has been looking for her since the day she left him, that he still loves her and that he isn't going away, because she is in danger, She loses all her fight and takes him back. Now that she has her man back all she has to do is, keep her mom and boss from killing him, keep herself from getting killed, and find out who put a hit on her head. Just another day in Cat's life!<br><br><b>"If anyone's under a spell, Justina, it's me. Your daughter put one on me five years ago, and I haven't broken free of it yet. Oh, and you'll be delighted to know, we've decided to resume our relationship. Don't bother with congratulations-trust me, your expression is congratulations enough."-Bones</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/bones%20and%20cat2_zpsizrwithb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><b>"But I'm not going to let you or anyone else decide what I do with my personal life anymore. You don't have to like Bones. Hell, you can hate his guts for all I care, but as long as I'm with him, you will have to tolerate him. So will Don and the others, or...or I'll leave and never come back."-Cat</b><br><br>Bones is the sexiest vampire ever! He was even better in this book. I loved how he handled Justina (Cat's mom). His love for Cat was unconditionally and unwavering. He fought for her, searched for her, and never gave up on her. I loved Bones jealous side, but I feel he acted like a saint, because I would have killed Tate. Cat was as bad ass as ever. I love that she really shows some growth in this book, standing up to everyone, and not letting them trash talk Bones, or all vampires in general. She has a confidence in this book that was just sexy. And a smart mouth that had me laughing hard.<br><br><b>"You know the old saying. Once you go dead, no one's better in bed."-Cat</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/tumblr_n0dk1bNtxh1rp4im3o1_500_zpsddwm7bgf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I couldn't stop shaking, especially when he kissed me and I tasted blood and other things on his tongue. "Oh, Kitten," he growled. "You have no idea how much I enjoyed that. I've already spilled myself inside you, bloody hell, I thought you'd castrate me with your pleasure. Do you know how long you've been whipping around from the effects of my bite?" Not a clue. "Five minutes?" To my shock, my voice was hoarse and nearly unrecognizable. He chuckled. "Try twenty, give or take a few. The police have already come and gone; Annette sent them away. I think the neighbors thought someone was being murdered."-Bones and Cat</b><br><br>I missed Bones so much in the parts of the book when he was out of the picture, but I still loved Cat so much that it didn't take away from my enjoyment of this book. That first time Bones said "Hallo Kitten" I squealed, bouncing up and down in my seat, clapping like a idoit yelling Yay Bones is back! Bones and Cat have such a strong connection. There is some ex drama in this book and of course Tate drama(Tate is one of Cat's team mates, but he is in love with her). OMG OMG OMG chapter 32. The sex in chapter 32 holy hell, it set my body on fire, melted my bones, made me start shaking, and left me basking in the afterglow. Fuck but that was the single best sex scene I have ever read ever. Ever! Bones is such a dirty naughty boy Dayum! I wanted to stab Bones's ex Annette and I was so happy when Cat beat the shit outta her and then of course stabbed her! <br><br><b>"I am going to knock the slut out of you, Annette," I gritted between clenched teeth. "And that should take some doing, you uppity English tramp!"-Cat<br><br><br>"I didn't miss, bitch. One flick of my wrist and you're a bad memory and an even worse smell. Then I knew I'd do anything to make you feel the same way."-Bones</b><br><br><br>Tons of action, amazing characters, and a great plot. I love this series and I can't wait to read the next one. <span id="freeTextContainer10082233991522365712"><b>4 1/2–Chapter 32! Need I Say More–Stars</b><br/><a href='http://s571.photobucket.com/user/kpeery1/media/Gifs/81682F6A-54FC-4414-B070-05274732EEC2.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>I love this book. I love Cat and Bones. They are quickly becoming one of my favorite paranormal couples. The only reason this book isn't a 5 star read is because I had a hard time staying engaged in the plot during the first 9 chapters. Frankly, I was bored out of my mind until the author stopped dragging out Bone's reappearance into the storyline. Other than that, <i>One Foot in the Grave</i> is a fantastic, enthralling, and sexy as sin read. </span>
  <span id="freeText10082233991522365712" style="display:none"><b>4 1/2–Chapter 32! Need I Say More–Stars</b><br><a href="http://s571.photobucket.com/user/kpeery1/media/Gifs/81682F6A-54FC-4414-B070-05274732EEC2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I love this book. I love Cat and Bones. They are quickly becoming one of my favorite paranormal couples. The only reason this book isn't a 5 star read is because I had a hard time staying engaged in the plot during the first 9 chapters. Frankly, I was bored out of my mind until the author stopped dragging out Bone's reappearance into the storyline. Other than that, <i>One Foot in the Grave</i> is a fantastic, enthralling, and sexy as sin read. </span>

<div id="review_125848364" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/125848364" />
    <a title="Kim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1594906-kim"><img alt="Kim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1252264728p2/1594906.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/125848364?book_show_action=true">Oct 11, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim" href="/user/show/1594906-kim">Kim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8129187-one-foot-in-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1594906-kim?shelf=read-in-2010">read-in-2010</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1594906-kim?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1594906-kim?shelf=ebook">ebook</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer125848364&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer125848364" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3791218691009501518">This will be just me ranting instead of writing a review. But it has a few spoilers.<br/><br/>We pick up the story 4 years after the events of Halfway To The Grave. Cat is now Commander Cat (lawl), and she leads a special government team. She broke up with Bones and hasn't seen him since. She was never subtle to begin with, but now Cat is so goddamn hot, it seems like everybody around her is constantly trying to get in her pants. In the first book, Bones provided enough distractions to keep things interes</span>
  <span id="freeText3791218691009501518" style="display:none">This will be just me ranting instead of writing a review. But it has a few spoilers.<br /><br />We pick up the story 4 years after the events of Halfway To The Grave. Cat is now Commander Cat (lawl), and she leads a special government team. She broke up with Bones and hasn't seen him since. She was never subtle to begin with, but now Cat is so goddamn hot, it seems like everybody around her is constantly trying to get in her pants. In the first book, Bones provided enough distractions to keep things interesting, but he's nowhere to be seen in the first half of the book. *yawns*<br /><br />Cat is bordering on pathetic; she took the same last name as her former lover, she got the same tattoo on her hip, she hasn't slept with anybody since Bones and she spends her days snapping nasty comments at people, and thinking of Bones and his tongue. Obviously she is completely oblivious to all the admirers she has, because that's what a Mary Sue is supposed to do, right? Tate has to spell it out for her. And even then she doesn't get it.<br /><br />The way Cat and Bones meet again is just one big followup of convenient plot devices. Cat has a best friend now, who gets married to a computer genius, completely out of the blue. (she is probably on honeymoon for the rest of the book because we don't hear from her again) And you already know this genius is going to be very useful some day (more like 10 chapters later). And you already know who is going to show up at the wedding. Only a massive amount of self-restraint causes Cat to keep herself in check when she sees Bones standing there in front of her, at the wedding. Which is completely out of character, since it's kind of her trademark. For example, when she meets the first vampire Bones made. Which is of course a woman. Who is in love with Bones. Who tries to scare Cat away by commenting on the massive amounts of sex they had over the past centuries. Result = Catfight.<br /><br />Of course, they hook up again, and then I finally got to read the famous Chapter 32 my friends kept talking about. WTF was up with that? I kept thinking about pigs, because <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/2941288-morgan-f" rel="nofollow noopener">Morgan</a>
</b> once told me they have 30-minute orgasms. That's pretty much what Cat went through for an entire night. With an audience. And with Bones boldly going where no man has ever gone before. Ick. I'm afraid to pick up the next book, because I'm positive the words 'golden' and 'shower' are going to pop up in the same sentence.<br /><br />I'm not saying I didn't have fun while I was reading this but there was just too much stupid in there. Things like Cat 'forgetting' she was half naked while she paraded around for everybody to see, the completely ridiculous impromptu marriage (basically they cut their hands, slapped them together and said "by my blood, let's do this shit"), the OMFGICANTLIVEWITHOUTYOU romance... That and about 409 other little things that got on my nerves. After a while I was thinking "If I see her 'palming' one more goddamn silver knife I'm going to slap a bitch. Because that's basically all she does, besides being a foulmouthed bitch to everybody and shagging Bones. Meh.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3791218691009501518" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_351649952" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/351649952" />
    <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow"><img alt="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1393785730p2/10336538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/351649952?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ " href="/user/show/10336538-jessica-silverbow">Jessica ❁ ➳ Silverbow ➳ ❁ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8129187-one-foot-in-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=jerk-of-my-dreams">jerk-of-my-dreams</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=not-your-ordinary-creatures">not-your-ordinary-creatures</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=favorite-secondary-characters">favorite-secondary-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=smut">smut</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10336538-jessica-silverbow?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer351649952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer207880608246579688">I don't know if Jeaniene Frost planned all along to do what she did in ONE FOOT IN THE GRAVE, the second installment of her NIGHT HUNTRESS series, or if she adapted after reader feedback . . . Either way, it was an excellent call. <br/><br/>In HALFWAY TO THE GRAVE, Cat Crawfield was slammed with many, many truths that grossly conflicted with her upbringing. She was distraught and confused, and rightfully so . . . <br/><br/>BUT.<br/><br/>As understandable as it was for Cat to struggle with her new worldview, it was also frust</span>
  <span id="freeText207880608246579688" style="display:none">I don't know if Jeaniene Frost planned all along to do what she did in ONE FOOT IN THE GRAVE, the second installment of her NIGHT HUNTRESS series, or if she adapted after reader feedback . . . Either way, it was an excellent call. <br><br>In HALFWAY TO THE GRAVE, Cat Crawfield was slammed with many, many truths that grossly conflicted with her upbringing. She was distraught and confused, and rightfully so . . . <br><br>BUT.<br><br>As understandable as it was for Cat to struggle with her new worldview, it was also frustrating and more than a wee bit tiresome.<br><br>So what do we do? <br><br><b>Fast forward four years.</b> *tips hat to Frost* *admires ingenuity*<br><br>Four years in which Cat has time to grow and mature, to accept herself and her abilities, to come to terms with her new reality.<br><br>It makes for an infinitely more likable Cat. <br><br>Oh, she's still not perfect. She's brash and executes secondary plans without a full grasp of the vampire world she's entering, but still . . . a <i>vast</i> improvement.<br><br>The cast of secondary characters is greatly expanded in addition to the character development of our old favorites. Justina in particular is as entertaining as she is conniving:<br><br><blockquote>
<i>My mother pulled me aside as soon as I left Noah. Her face was florid. <br>“Do you know what that beast did when you walked away from him at the bar? He </i>winked<i> at me!” <br>Caught off guard, I laughed. God, that was priceless. She must have had steam coming out of her ears. <br>“You think that’s funny?” she irrationally demanded. <br>“Well, Mom, he risked his life for you, and then you tried your damnedest to have him killed. He may not like you.”</i>
</blockquote><br>As for the plot . . . *grins evilly* . . . it was FANGTASTIC. <br><br>When last we saw Cat, she was forced to leave Bones. To protect him. To protect her mother (stupid cow). Misguided as she was, she had good reasons for slinking away the second his back was turned. <br><br>But this is Bones. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445347311ra/16636416.gif" width="360" height="169" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He's not going to let her go without a fight, and, man alive, their reunion is . . . so much fun. It's horrible, really. Mortifying for Cat on so many (deserved) levels, but so, so fun. <br><br>And as random as what brought them together was, it was excellent timing. Cat had a run in with Bone's sire who now sought to add her to his collection of rare and beautiful things. <br><br>Like a painting. For his wall.<br><br>Bastard. <br><br>Then there's the night before the big confrontation . . . If you're familiar with this series, you know what I'm talking about. The night when Bones is determined to show Cat that he wants no one but her . . . The night where he DOESTHETHING.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411926476ra/11300873.gif" width="380" height="186" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's probably the single hottest vampire sex scene I've ever read. *loins are aflame*<br><br>SO. A definite improvement that I highly (HIGHLY) recommend. *fans self* *is useless* *doesn't care*</span>
  <a data-text-id="207880608246579688" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1308139215" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3437790937478387861"><b>BONES DOES IT AGAIN!!</b> <br/><br/>Bones has some of the most humorous lines I’ve ever read in paranormal romance books. But I have to hand it to Cat because she had the best line in the whole book:<br/><br/><b>“You know that old saying. Once you go dead, no one's better in bed.” </b> <br/><br/>I love Bones & Cat together because I know I'm in for a fun adventure. My only fault I had with this story was the beginning of the book because it lacked Bones. I found myself struggling to stay interested in what was happening with the plot l</span>
  <span id="freeText3437790937478387861" style="display:none"><b>BONES DOES IT AGAIN!!</b> <br><br>Bones has some of the most humorous lines I’ve ever read in paranormal romance books. But I have to hand it to Cat because she had the best line in the whole book:<br><br><b>“You know that old saying. Once you go dead, no one's better in bed.” </b> <br><br>I love Bones &amp; Cat together because I know I'm in for a fun adventure. My only fault I had with this story was the beginning of the book because it lacked Bones. I found myself struggling to stay interested in what was happening with the plot line. Once Bones showed up I was all in. <br><br>I listened to this one and was a little weirded out that the <i>voice</i> for Noah is the same voice the narrator used for a different book: Flat Out Celeste (Justin). I’m glad he didn’t play a very big role in the book because it was off putting to hear that voice and think of Justin from the other book.<br><br>Overall I enjoyed the audio and found myself entertained when Bones was calling the shots. Now that I'm hooked on the series I can't wait to get my hands on the next installment in Night Huntress series.<br><br><b>SERIES:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1421990.Halfway_to_the_Grave__Night_Huntress___1_" title="Halfway to the Grave (Night Huntress, #1) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3570231.At_Grave_s_End__Night_Huntress___3_" title="At Grave's End (Night Huntress, #3) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1330786048s/3570231.jpg" alt="At Grave's End (Night Huntress, #3) by Jeaniene Frost" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

</a><br>Ms. Frost has a recommended reading order that can be found <a href="http://jeanienefrost.com/reading-order/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>.<br><br><i>Novellas:</i><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10822857.Reckoning__Night_Huntress___0_5_" title="Reckoning (Night Huntress, #0.5) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1984401502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1984401502" />
    <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews"><img alt="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1492999740p2/66199133.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1984401502?book_show_action=true">Apr 27, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀" href="/user/show/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews">Cece ❀Rants, Raves &amp;Reviews❀</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=reviews-of-the-year">reviews-of-the-year</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=favorite-heroine">favorite-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=nothing-else-2-read">nothing-else-2-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=hot-jerks">hot-jerks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/66199133-cece-rants-raves-reviews?shelf=magic-etc">magic-etc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1984401502" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4912779228644495180"><b>For a second book, I wanted....</b>better secondary characters, more Cat and Bones: fight fight fight kiss kiss kiss, the mom to die, and what happened to Timmie? #the real MVP<br/><br/>Overall this second book did pretty well on delivering <b>but it left a Timmie-shaped hole in my heart.</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605732.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So Cat is working for the government: <b>stabbing people and getting paid for it.</b> A regular white-collar, tax paying job. But without boy-toy Bones, she is lonely and there's some friend who just hangs around and tells her to get s</span>
  <span id="freeText4912779228644495180" style="display:none"><b>For a second book, I wanted....</b>better secondary characters, more Cat and Bones: fight fight fight kiss kiss kiss, the mom to die, and what happened to Timmie? #the real MVP<br><br>Overall this second book did pretty well on delivering <b>but it left a Timmie-shaped hole in my heart.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605732.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So Cat is working for the government: <b>stabbing people and getting paid for it.</b> A regular white-collar, tax paying job. But without boy-toy Bones, she is lonely and there's some friend who just hangs around and tells her to get some *smh* <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605733.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Dazzle Noah with your drinking skills, burn his ears with your language, but try to have a little fun with a guy you’re not intending to kill by the end of the night"</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> I had some high hopes for <b>Denise</b>, her introduction into the supernatural world really set up some great possibilites: <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“To her credit, she hadn’t screamed, fainted, or done any of the things a normal person would. She’d simply blinked and said, “Wow. I owe you a beer, at least.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>However, their friendship together <b>was explained rather than shown</b> I wanted more bonding between the two, so whatever.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605734.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Cat's character definitely matured more, realizing the dangerous positions from the first book and being more cautious: <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I slept with one of my knives under my bed, telling myself I wasn’t being paranoid. I was just being cautious. Yeah, right. I didn’t believe it, either.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>But for all you <b>violent lovers</b> that needs a heroine threatening to beat people up all the time, <b>don't you worry your lil butt</b> <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“Her prim tone made me squeeze my glass so hard to avoid slamming it over her head that it shattered”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>So of course <b>Bones </b> tracks her down at the agency and was somehow both extremely helpful and aggravating at the same time. <u>~Like I'm helping you but it aint for you sweetie...? ~</u><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605735.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I have been stabbed, shot, burned, bitten, beaten unconscious too many times to count, and even staked. None of those held a candle to the pain I felt at seeing his mouth on hers.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br> This book also <i>*thankfully*</i> answered some of questions about Bones, ooo backstory. Plus it entertaining as they were both trying to figure out their place within the vampires society together. <br><br><b>The first book literally revolved around Cat and Bones stabbing the shit out of vamps.</b> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605736.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Other characters only had importance if Cat and Bones were fighting them and that was it. <br><br>As such that first book, had a vibe of the <b>vampires being college frat-boys</b> where vamps all went to clubs to get drunk and feed off of humans. It was fine for the first book <b>but lets be honest: some vamps have been alive for hundreds of years, I'm sure someone got their shit together .</b><br><br>Well lo and behold: this book delivered with wayyy more sophisticated societies and <b>vampires who weren't there just to get stabbed *whoaaaa* </b> <u>Annette</u> being the main one who was part of Bone's pastttttt..... <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A catfight, no pun intended. Annette said some nasty things and so did I, and then i stabbed her to make a point. Now that was a pun.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605737.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>One of the best scenes was definitely Annette vs Cat followed by a clean-up afterwards where Annette <i>" became blur of cleaning motion, like Martha Stewart on crack cocaine.”</i> Lol <br><br><b>Now enter angry Bones:</b> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“And that, Annette, is called Pilates,” I said, giving an exaggerated stretch.<br>“Very entertaining,” she hastened to agree, turning blameless eyes to him”<br>“Unless Pilates has become downright lethal, I’d say the two of you were fighting.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>One thing I definitely noticed was the <b>improvements on secondary characters.</b> They were more 3D and some of them were pretty funny/interesting so it added to general story. <b>Juan, Tate , Dave, and Don</b>. This group of guys were pretty hilarious- training, stabbing, and shamelessly flirting with each other. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1493342998ra/22605738.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The banter between them was pretty great at times <blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“You called her Kitten? And she let you? She put me in a coma for three days when i called her that! My balls never recovered from her smashing them into my spine!”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><b>But not quite the same as the first.</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1471807179ra/20109627.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br> *side note there was wayyy 2 much "mommy issues" in here* <br><br>Then of course <b> some great lesson in the end</b> that Cat ironically teaches even though the first book was about beating this very thought into her stubborn head..? <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474463250ra/20603059.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“... overcome an unexpected heritage. We are who we make ourselves to be, no matter what. No matter what. You’re still you. You’ll still laugh, cry, do your job, lose at poker…</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>For a sequel it wasn't bad. An entertaining read, I'll definitely keep reading because the characters are entertaining as *fuck* and the plot seems to keep building up. This is less of a paranormal detective and more of a paranormal assassin. I dig it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4912779228644495180" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Shawna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna"><img alt="Shawna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574172018p2/1802746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/40404777?book_show_action=true">Dec 18, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shawna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shawna" href="/user/show/1802746-shawna">Shawna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Hot vampire lovers; PNR and urban fantasy fans</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=pnr-vampires">pnr-vampires</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame">hero-stud-mantel-hall-of-fame</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=heroine-i-adore">heroine-i-adore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=a-all-time-favorite-hero">a-all-time-favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=2009-reads">2009-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=hero-i-wanna-marry">hero-i-wanna-marry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1802746-shawna?shelf=badasses-hunks-in-leather">badasses-hunks-in-leather</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40404777" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16558068707729134964">5++ stars – Vampire Romance/Urban Fantasy<br/><br/>WOW...just WOW! I loved, loved, loved this book! Cat and Bones are back with bite in <i>One Foot in the Grave</i>, and as amazing as the first book was, this one’s even better.<br/><br/>Cat’s kick-ass vampire slaying is ramped up much higher this go round, and we also get a nice appetizingly, mouth-wateringly luscious, juicy Bones fix that had me melting like an ice cream cone on a hot summer day...Y-U-M! There’s lots of fast paced, high-octane action, witty laugh-out-lou</span>
  <span id="freeText16558068707729134964" style="display:none">5++ stars – Vampire Romance/Urban Fantasy<br /><br />WOW...just WOW! I loved, loved, loved this book! Cat and Bones are back with bite in <i>One Foot in the Grave</i>, and as amazing as the first book was, this one’s even better.<br /><br />Cat’s kick-ass vampire slaying is ramped up much higher this go round, and we also get a nice appetizingly, mouth-wateringly luscious, juicy Bones fix that had me melting like an ice cream cone on a hot summer day...Y-U-M! There’s lots of fast paced, high-octane action, witty laugh-out-loud humor, sarcastic, hilarious dialogue, an uproariously fun catfight, and smokin’ hot romance, including one delectably erotic sex scene that almost necessitated calling the fire department to hose me down when I nearly burst into flames! Seriously, it’s one of the hottest scenes I’ve ever read because it consists of some very delicious, tantalizing possibilities/fantasies (fangs included) of having a doting vampire for a lover whose sole desire is to deliver ultimate, exquisite pleasure. Bones is flat-out one of the sexiest, most deliciously yummy bad-boy romantic heroes ever, and he definitely rivals and exceeds Edward and The Brothers for my very top favorite, hottest vamp! Marry me, Bones!!!!<br /><br />Here are a couple of funny quotes from the book that I liked: <br /><br />Cat chasing down a vamp, (page 111)<br /><br />...“cursing my heels and debating whether it was faster to stop and take them off--damn ankle straps!--or keep running with the potential neck breakers. Wouldn’t that make a charming epitaph? <i>Here lies Cat. Killed not by fang, but Ferragamos</i>.”<br /><br />Bones trying to prove that Cat still has feelings for him, (page 112)<br /><br />“It was if you were sending me a bloomin’ valentine.”<br /><br />So if you like bad-ass, butt-kicking heroines, uber sexy vampire heroes, and a fun paranormal/urban fantasy romance with a terrific mix of thrilling action, dark humor, and hot sex, give Cat and Bones a read...you won’t be disappointed! Verrry big 5 stars!<br /><br />*One of my very top favorite PNR reads ever!<br />*A top favorite PNR series!<br />*Cat and Bones are my favorite romance/PNR couple!<br />*Bones is my all time #1 top favorite hot bad-boy vampire hero!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16558068707729134964" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2184949207" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2184949207" />
    <a title="Sophia Triad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad"><img alt="Sophia Triad" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591419108p2/44642860.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2184949207?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sophia Triad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sophia Triad" href="/user/show/44642860-sophia-triad">Sophia Triad</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=1paranormal-lovestories">1paranormal-lovestories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=vampires">vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44642860-sophia-triad?shelf=ghouls">ghouls</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2184949207" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2788572332337943368">4 years ago, Bones made a promise (a threat? a friendly reminder?):<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“If you run from me, I will chase you, and I'll find you....”</i>

  <span id="freeText2788572332337943368" style="display:none">4 years ago, Bones made a promise (a threat? a friendly reminder?):<br /><br /><b>

They were together for just a few months, but she still loves him. Now she has an important job to do in the Homeland Security Paranormal department. Not very different to the one she used to do when she was working with Bones. She still plays the role of bait in missions in order to catch bad vampires. Having a beating heart, nobody suspects that she is half vampire.<br /><br />Fate will bring Bones back to her. When Cat’s best friend gets married, Cat will be surprised to learn that the best man is Bones.<br /><br />Bones and Cat “shockingly” (yeah right) will be together again, but this time there will also be lots of jealously in their relationship. <br /><br />There will be Annette drama.<br />There will be Tate drama.<br /><br />Cat will prove to be a badass possessive half-vampire (<b>

He chuckled.<br />"Try twenty, give or take a few. The police have already come and gone; Annette sent them away. I think the neighbors thought someone was being murdered."</i>

<span id="freeTextContainer13277979681585767459">A good read, but nowhere near as gripping and emotionally involving as the first Night Huntress installment.<br/><br/>I had tons of fun readng One Foot in the Grave because of the wit, snarkiness, and generally funny moments all over the book. This one resembled the last book in that way. I've picked out some of my favorite quotes/passages:<br/><i>
  <blockquote>"Life's a bitch and then one stabs you."</blockquote>
  <br/>
  <blockquote>Just like old times, I thought ironically. I look like a slut, and Bones is my backup while I go after murdering fang-b</blockquote></i></span>
  <span id="freeText13277979681585767459" style="display:none">A good read, but nowhere near as gripping and emotionally involving as the first Night Huntress installment.<br /><br />I had tons of fun readng One Foot in the Grave because of the wit, snarkiness, and generally funny moments all over the book. This one resembled the last book in that way. I've picked out some of my favorite quotes/passages:<br /><i>
  <blockquote>"Life's a bitch and then one stabs you."</blockquote>
  <br />
  <blockquote>Just like old times, I thought ironically. I look like a slut, and Bones is my backup while I go after murdering fang-bangers. The only thing that would make this complete would be to take off my underwear. <br />Then I smiled. And went back into the stall.</blockquote>
  <br />
  <blockquote>"You know the old saying. Once you go dead, no one's better in bed."</blockquote>
  <br />
  <blockquote>"What's next? You going to whip out a dick and say you're really a man?"</blockquote>
  <br />
  <blockquote>"Wrong way, Bones. The men's showers are in the oppostie direction."<br />"I'll file that away with all the other information that doesn't pertain to me."</blockquote>
  <br />
  <blockquote>"You will pay with pain for that."<br />What was I supposed to say? It wasn't good for me, either?</blockquote>
</i><br />So needless to say I laughed a lot in the process of reading. This book made me very happy. <br /><br />However I did have some issues with it. For one, Cat slut-shames a lady at a wedding, and I can't stand people who slut-shame. How can women do that to each other? I expected better from Cat.<br /><br />My biggest problem was Bones and Cat's relationship. Even after spending 4 years apart, when they meet again it's like nothing can ever bring them apart again. I'm glad Cat and Bones are so perfect for one another, but it doesn't motivate me to keep reading. If no obstacle can create serious conflict in their relationship, then why should I read about it? No conflict = nothing driving the plot = nothing to interest me. I could just congratulate Cat and Bones on their perfect love lives and move on to a different series.</span>

<div id="review_161016347" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/161016347" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/161016347?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Anyone who loved Spike half as much as I did</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2011">2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer161016347" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6053664834058010024"><b>EDIT:</b> I'm adding a honorary star to the first two books in this series, just because Frost has been consistently awesome throughout.<br/><br/>I really really enjoyed this book but I just can't quite bring myself to award it 5 stars when you compare it to, say, Margaret Atwood's genius in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38447' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Handmaid's Tale</a> or the deeply entwined mystery/romance/mythology of <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750' rel='nofollow noopener'>Darkfever</a> and the rest of the Fever series. This is an easy-to-read addictive series with a heroine who is likeable, brave (without being unrealistic</span>
  <span id="freeText6053664834058010024" style="display:none"><b>EDIT:</b> I'm adding a honorary star to the first two books in this series, just because Frost has been consistently awesome throughout.<br /><br />I really really enjoyed this book but I just can't quite bring myself to award it 5 stars when you compare it to, say, Margaret Atwood's genius in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/38447" rel="nofollow noopener">The Handmaid's Tale</a> or the deeply entwined mystery/romance/mythology of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/112750" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkfever</a> and the rest of the Fever series. This is an easy-to-read addictive series with a heroine who is likeable, brave (without being unrealistically so), and pretty much always horny. That last point being awesome when you have a sexy character like Bones as the love interest.<br /><br />People may say Bones is a complete rip-off of Spike from <i>Buffy</i>, and they're right - he is. But since when did that become a bad thing? Spike is the one true love of my media-saturated heart and Bones does everything he did, says most words and phrases that he said (sodding, shagging, bloody hell) and has a lot of hot, kinky sex like Spike also did with Buffy :D Not to mention the fact that he is a <i>very</i> selfless bed partner. Still, I don't feel right giving 5 stars to a novel that is, when all things are said and done, just a really good and really smutty <i>Buffy</i> fanfic.<br /><br />But I do also like the way Bones can be caring without having to play the over-protective male. It happens all the time in paranormal romance that the girl's weaknesses are played upon and in swoops Mr gorgeous-and-usually-dead to save the day. But in this series, Cat and Bones are a team, working to watch out for one another without it being one-sided; and Bones never underestimates Cat's ability or judgement. You may be guessing by now that I sort of really love Bones.<br /><br />What this book claims to be and just isn't that much is Urban Fantasy - the lines tend to blend between UF and paranomal romance sometimes but this series is definitely the latter of the two, regardless of what the library sections try to say it is. It is heavily focused on character relationships and sex, not that this is a bad thing in my opinion but the bad guy (or girl) of the moment often gets put on the back burner in favour of the protagonist's sex life. Like I said before - smutty fanfic.<br /><br />So this book, in fact this series, is not perfect. I could complain on and on about the story not being particularly great because Frost focuses her energy on what Bones can do with chains and blindfolds (the answer - <i>a lot</i>), but what would really be the point when I enjoyed reading this so much. Goodreads' rating system doesn't offer opinion on quality of plot or writing in particular, just "liked it", "really liked it" and so on... well, yeah, I really liked it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6053664834058010024" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1643501507?book_show_action=true">May 20, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22189348-adina?shelf=urban-fantasy-pr">urban-fantasy-pr</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1643501507" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13907150658179515666">I read this terrible follow-up to the dreadful vampire novel, Halfway to the Grave a few weeks ago while I had my brain locked by a sad event. I could only read this kind of books, where any sign of intelligence from my part was not needed. <br/><br/>I do enjoy these kind of books from time to time so no problem there. What is inexcusable is that I considered to be a good idea putting myself again through the pain of reading this series. More cheesy love declarations, stupid jealously, bad action sequence</span>
  <span id="freeText13907150658179515666" style="display:none">I read this terrible follow-up to the dreadful vampire novel, Halfway to the Grave a few weeks ago while I had my brain locked by a sad event. I could only read this kind of books, where any sign of intelligence from my part was not needed. <br /><br />I do enjoy these kind of books from time to time so no problem there. What is inexcusable is that I considered to be a good idea putting myself again through the pain of reading this series. More cheesy love declarations, stupid jealously, bad action sequences. Even the “infamous” sex scene that all the reviews were raving about was a bit meh. Vampire juice, really?? <br /><br />I understand that the sexy bits are the most important parts of a paranormal romance but I also expect an interesting story, something that does not make me want to puke. <br /><br />No more from this author, no more. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13907150658179515666" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_28922623" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/28922623" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/28922623?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Any paranormal fan, but especially fans of JR Ward and Kresley Cole</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2009_reads">2009_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=husband-worthy_hero">husband-worthy_hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer28922623" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15483720106310510484"><i>The</i> most reading fun I've had all year! Can I give this book more than 5 stars? This book has it all--the totally unique characters, the imaginative story line, the ultra witty dialogue, the set-the-sheets-on-fire bedroom action, the kick a** heroine, and the number one, sexiest bad-boy 'Master' vampire of all time, the swoon-worthy Bones! Oh my, he may have just replaced Rhage as my all-time favorite vamp! God, the things he says and does...words cannot describe his utter hotness...to try to do</span>
  <span id="freeText15483720106310510484" style="display:none"><i>The</i> most reading fun I've had all year! Can I give this book more than 5 stars? This book has it all--the totally unique characters, the imaginative story line, the ultra witty dialogue, the set-the-sheets-on-fire bedroom action, the kick a** heroine, and the number one, sexiest bad-boy 'Master' vampire of all time, the swoon-worthy Bones! Oh my, he may have just replaced Rhage as my all-time favorite vamp! God, the things he says and does...words cannot describe his utter hotness...to try to do so would do him a disservice.:)<br /><br />This book was just jam packed with goodies from the start with nary a slow spot. Half vamp/half human Cat and vampire bounty hunter/former gigolo Bones are temporarily broken up (I never thought it would last <i>4 years!</i>--how could she keep herself from him for <i>4 years</i>?) but the way Bones comes back into her life (*sigh*) you know that Cat doesn't stand a chance in hell of resisting him! Cat has a whole new career working for the government as a Special Agent (complete with her own team of men--who all deserve their own books, btw), ridding the world of some really unsavory vampires. There's lots of grisly battles, but Cat's a tough, cool customer, and can handle <i>anything</i>, except when it comes to her feelings for Bones. And once he steps back into her life you know she's toast.<br /><br />There's lots of violence and some grisly scenes involving some bad vamps (I'm in awe of Jeaniene Frost's wicked imagination), but there's no skimping on the romance. The pages just come alive whenever Cat and Bones are together, and the big romantic scene when Cat tells Bones to not hold back and that she wants all that he can give her...<i>whew</i>...have plenty of ice ready, because you're going to need it! Hot, hot, <b>HOT!!</b><br /><br />I loved the cat fight (no pun intended) between Cat and the first vamp that Bones 'made', the Susan Sarandon look-alike and devilishly skanky Annette--go Cat, put that b**** in her place! I loved the remark that Cat made to her teammate Tate (who has an annoyingly mad crush on her) while defending her relationship with Bones--<i>"Once you go dead, no one's better in bed."</i> This book was filled with those witty remarks, icluding this one from Bones to Cat...<i>"Hallo, luv. Long time no taste."</i>:)<br /><br />And finally, I loved how the book built and built until the final showdown between Cat and her long lost Daddy vamp, and the vamp who originally 'made' Bones--awesome fight scene that had me on pins and needles and outrageously witty dialogue. And just when you think you've read it all and had enough, Frost throws a big fat curveball at the end and provides some more "ghoulish' entertainment that would make Stephen King proud!<br /><br />Well, I could go on and on about all the entertaining sequences in this book, but what I <i>loved</i> the most was the staggering love between Bones and Cat--they are without a doubt my favorite paranormal romance couple. I just can't get enough of them--they are scorchingly hot! I don't know what else Jeaniene Frost has in store for them, but I'm ready. Bring on <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3570231.At_Grave_s_End__Night_Huntress___3_" title="At Grave's End (Night Huntress, #3) by Jeaniene Frost" rel="nofollow noopener">At Grave's End</a>! 5 big stars!</span>
  <a data-text-id="15483720106310510484" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_759299428" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/759299428" />
    <a title="Shelly Strange" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange"><img alt="Shelly Strange" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600285315p2/25393430.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/759299428?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelly Strange" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelly Strange" href="/user/show/25393430-shelly-strange">Shelly Strange</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-urban">fantasy-urban</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-2015">read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=hot-guys-alphas-rawr">hot-guys-alphas-rawr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=read-more-than-once">read-more-than-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25393430-shelly-strange?shelf=fantasy-vampires">fantasy-vampires</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer759299428" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12327325926544543555"><b>First read: May 2014: ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ <br/>Second read: April 2015: ★ ★ ★ </b><br/><br/>Well, I definitely don't think this is a 5 star book anymore. My tastes and standards have changed a lot just in one year!<br/><br/>The first half of this book is basically what has Cat been up to in the 4 years she blew off Bones and joined a secret government group that hunts rogue vampires who kill humans. Cat is their leader and thought she was saving Bones' life by leaving him and disappearing. YAWN. <br/><br/>I never liked the secret military stor</span>
  <span id="freeText12327325926544543555" style="display:none"><b>First read: May 2014: ★ ★ ★ ★ ★ <br />Second read: April 2015: ★ ★ ★ </b><br /><br />Well, I definitely don't think this is a 5 star book anymore. My tastes and standards have changed a lot just in one year!<br /><br />The first half of this book is basically what has Cat been up to in the 4 years she blew off Bones and joined a secret government group that hunts rogue vampires who kill humans. Cat is their leader and thought she was saving Bones' life by leaving him and disappearing. YAWN. <br /><br />I never liked the secret military storyline. All the characters there are one-dimensional. There's Juan, the cute Latino who only thinks about sex and always says "Madre de Dios!" There's Tate, the angry, hard-nosed military special forces type. <br /><br />The first half is all about relationship angst. Cat is dating some guy named Noah. (Who cares, seriously? This is just filler for when Bones comes back.) Then, Bones <i>does</i> come back and Cat gets all angsty and annoying. Like we don't know they will get back together. <br /><br />Cat slut-shames someone in this book, just like she did in the first one. I blame that on the author. There are a lot of romance stereotypes in this series. I felt like a lot of the first half was manufactured drama and unnecessary.<br /><br />The second half was better. I liked the action and story. Bones is a bad-ass. I just don't know what he sees in Cat, really. Here's another PNR trope... the ancient alpha male is mysteriously drawn to the inexperienced, hot, young female and they fall insta-madly in love. Bones tells Cat he loved her the first time they met. Really. Why? It doesn't make sense. <br /><br />I think I just expect more these days and it's hard for me to overlook these annoying themes that are repeated over and over in romances. Ugh.<br /><br /><b>Re-read starting 10 April 2015 with a few of my friends at the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles</a> group. YAY! I can always use a good Bones fix.</b><br /><br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="12327325926544543555" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2077142853" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2077142853" />
    <a title="Jilly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25894509-jilly"><img alt="Jilly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1435955932p2/25894509.jpg" /></a>

<div id="review_2272875383" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2272875383" />
    <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books"><img alt="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415550632p2/5892196.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2272875383?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)" href="/user/show/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books">Carole (Carole&#39;s Random Life in Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/32385243-one-foot-in-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=purchased">purchased</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=2018">2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5892196-carole-carole-s-random-life-in-books?shelf=series">series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2272875383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17690480808697966952">This review can also be found at <a href='http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br/><br/>I am having a lot of fun with my audio re-read of this series. It has been a little more than five years since I read this book the first time so it was definitely time to revisit this wonderful story. This was a book that once I really got into the story, I didn't want to put it down. I ended up listening to the whole audiobook in just a couple of days and I think I liked the book even more the second time around.<br/><br/>I do have to admit </span>
  <span id="freeText17690480808697966952" style="display:none">This review can also be found at <a href="http://carolesrandomlife.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Carole's Random Life in Books</a>.<br /><br />I am having a lot of fun with my audio re-read of this series. It has been a little more than five years since I read this book the first time so it was definitely time to revisit this wonderful story. This was a book that once I really got into the story, I didn't want to put it down. I ended up listening to the whole audiobook in just a couple of days and I think I liked the book even more the second time around.<br /><br />I do have to admit that I had a bit of a rough start with this book. This book begins several years after the events of the previous book where Cat left Bones to protect him. She is working her government job that she took to protect her mother at the end of the first book. She is very good at her job and has a good team working around her. <br /><br />I learned something very important while listening to this book. I like Bones a whole lot more than I like Cat. So much more. Bones wasn't around for the first part of this book so it was all Cat. I missed Bones. A lot. As soon as Bones entered the story again, my enjoyment increased dramatically. If you had asked me a year ago, I would have told you that I loved Cat and Bones. I discovered that I do love Bones but Cat has the potential to drive me a little crazy at times. Maybe by the end of my re-read of the series, I will love her just as much as Bones.<br /><br />There are quite a few really important developments in this book. Bones and Cat are reunited which is a very good thing. Cat is in some danger which is not so good but Bones is able to help keep her safe since he is back in her life. We do also get to meet some other important characters including Cat's team and some of Bone's friends and acquaintances. There are some pretty intense action scenes and some scenes that are more than a little hot. <br /><br />Tavia Gilbert does such a great job with this series. She really brings both Cat and Bones to life. I love the voice that she used for Bones and think that the accent is perfect. All of the characters are very easy to distinguish with each voice used being unique and very believable. She handled a wide range of emotions and a lot of different types of scenes with ease in this book. I had no trouble listening to this book for hours at a time.<br /><br />I do highly recommend this series to others. This is the second book in the Night Huntress series which really should be read in order since each book builds on previous events. I can't wait to continue my re-read of this amazing series!<br /><br /><b>Initial Thoughts</b><br />I had fun with this one. I had a bit of a rough start with it though. I found that I am a much bigger fan of Bones than I am of Cat and Bones was absent during the first part of the book. Even when Bones was back in the story, Cat still drove me nuts at times with her actions and jealous behavior. Don't get me wrong...I still had a great time with it. Tavia Gilbert did a fantastic job with the narration.<br /><br />Book source: Audible purchase</span>
  <a data-text-id="17690480808697966952" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
