<span id="freeTextContainer5114336420427157406"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Bones is awesome*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 06.11.2018</u>
</b><br/>The second book in the series starts with over a four years gap since the previous book ended. Half-vampire <b>Catherine ‘Cat’ ‘Cathy’ ‘Kitten’ ‘Commander’ ‘The Red Reaper’ Kathleen Crawfield</b> (27) is now working for the government after making a deal with them. The only one who know who she really is vampire bounty hunter/hit man <b>Crispin Phillip Arthur Russell III</b> (Crispin was his human name) <b>‘Bones’</b> (245? 246?), who Cat left behind in</span>
  <span id="freeText5114336420427157406" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱*Bones is awesome*⋰⋱⋰⋱⋰⋱</b>
</blockquote><br><b>
  <u>Second re-read: 06.11.2018</u>
</b><br>The second book in the series starts with over a four years gap since the previous book ended. Half-vampire <b>Catherine ‘Cat’ ‘Cathy’ ‘Kitten’ ‘Commander’ ‘The Red Reaper’ Kathleen Crawfield</b> (27) is now working for the government after making a deal with them. The only one who know who she really is vampire bounty hunter/hit man <b>Crispin Phillip Arthur Russell III</b> (Crispin was his human name) <b>‘Bones’</b> (245? 246?), who Cat left behind in order to save him. After all, they can't really have a future together. However, love is hard to get rid of, specially when one refuses to move on. <b>Overall, it's a awesome</b> - not the best though - book in the series. On to the next one! Oh and I love how <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Cat and Bones are now married in the vampire world. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Miss. Cristine Russell.” That was the name I went under now, another tribute to my lost love, since Bones’s human name had been Crispin Russell. My sentimental curse would be the end of me.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Other Character</u>:</b><br>→ <b>Justina Crawfield</b>, Cat's mother.<br>→ <b>Baron Charles ‘Spade’ DeMortimer</b>, Bones' best friend.<br>→ <b>Liam Flannery</b> aka <b>Ian</b> (over 200), Bones and Spade's shire/master.<br>→ <b>Rodney</b>, a ghoul and friend of Bones.<br>→ <b>Donald ‘Don’ Williams</b> (around 50), the head of a unit in the FBI called the Paranormal Behavior Division; a combination of CIA, FBI, and the armed forces. He's Cat's boss. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Turns out that he's Cat's uncle; her mother's rapist's brother (Max). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Tate Bradley</b> (late twenties), had been a sergeant in the Special Forces, a very select unit of them, is now on Cat's team. He's Cat's second-in-command.<br>→ <b>Dave</b> and <b>Juan</b>, Cat's other two captains. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Dave gets killed by a vampire and at end of the book, Rodney and Bones make him a ghoul. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>→ <b>Denise</b>, Cat's friend for over three years. Cat saved her from a vampire. <b>Randy</b>, who becomes her husband.<br>→ <b>Cooper</b>, a new member of Cat's team (2 months), he’s smart, fast, and ruthless. His years as an undercover narcotics officer probably helped there. He’s performed well in training operations, so they are now trying to see how he does in the field. He doesn’t like Cat; thinks she’ll turn on them one day because she a half-breed. He becomes Cat's third captain.<br>→ <b>Mencheres</b> (looks no older than 30), the vampire who made Ian, so that makes him Bones' fang granddaddy/grandsire. He’s a very powerful vampire who Ian wouldn’t want to cross. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Since Cat's father, <b>Maximillian ‘Max’</b>, is a member of Ian’s line and still under his protection, any attack against Max would be the same as an attack against Ian in the vampire world. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Mencheres sees things; visions, glimpses of the future, that sort. It’s one of his powers. He can also read humans’ minds, and it seems, half-breeds, too (but not vampires’ minds).<br>→ <b>Annette</b>, the first vampire Bones had ever made. She had help him when Bones was human, and Bones wanted to return the favor; to become a vampire, she accepted.<br>→ Dr. <b>Noah Rose</b>, a vet who starts dating Cat.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You’re dating a vampire! You just admitted it!” Tate burst out.<br>I shrugged. “You know the old saying. Once you go dead, no one’s better in bed.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><u>Quick basic facts</u>:</b><br><b>Genre</b>: - (Adult) Paranormal Romance/Urban Fantasy?.<br><b>Series</b>: - Series, Book Two.<br><b>Love triangle?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Cheating?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>HEA?</b> - <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[No. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><b>Favorite character?</b> - Bones.<br><b>Would I read more by this author/or of series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Would I recommend this book/series?</b> - Yes.<br><b>Will I read this again in the future?</b> - Probably.<br><b>New Rating</b> - 3.5/4 stars.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Re-read: 19.04.15</b><br>Bones is amazing.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445268775i/16623124.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b><u>First read review</u>:</b><br>On to the third one! Can't get enough of Bones!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer827261188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5863584143660470224"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4 "HOLY CHAPTER 32" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390265338ra/8179432.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>“This isn’t going to be easy,” I grumbled as we headed toward the exit. <br/><br/>Bones shrugged. “Nothing worthwhile ever is.” <br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br/>I couldn't wait to start this one! I had been told that Chapter 32 would blow my mind! And it did! I seriously want Bones so bad! <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='405' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's been four years, that right FOUR years (I was surprised myself), since Cat left Bones to become a secret a</span>
  <span id="freeText5863584143660470224" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380400128i/775030._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4 "HOLY CHAPTER 32" STARS ♥♥♥</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1390265338ra/8179432.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“This isn’t going to be easy,” I grumbled as we headed toward the exit. <br><br>Bones shrugged. “Nothing worthwhile ever is.” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote><br>I couldn't wait to start this one! I had been told that Chapter 32 would blow my mind! And it did! I seriously want Bones so bad! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's been four years, that right FOUR years (I was surprised myself), since Cat left Bones to become a secret agent for the government that deals with paranormal cases. By now, everyone has heard about the "Red Reaper", and as a result, someone is trying to have her assasinated. Her team is not enough to keep her safe. Then Bones finds her, and wants to do whatever he can to help her. She doesn't think she can be near him, especially when he gets her all hot and bothered with his mere presence. She agrees anyways. But that also brings exes into the mix which in turn brings jealousy. (So, you know it's gonna be good, right?)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390264465i/8179218._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You know I still care about you, obviously, but it's more than tat. I'm...I still love you. I've never stopped, actually, even though I tried to snap out of it over the years. I don't expect you to feel the same way, but-"<br><br>"I've never stopped loving you. Not for an instant. Even when I was so angry at you for leaving me, I've always loved you, Kitten."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote>Cat was still the kickass vampire hunter Bones taught her to be. But just like in the first book, I had trouble liking her at first. She actually annoyed me quite a bit in some scenes, I think more so than the first. But by the end of it, I managed to like her again. I feel for her, because of her crazy annoying as hell mother. She still hates vampires and I REALLY hope that it one day changes. How can she possibly hate Bones?? I just don't get it, especially when he constantly shows how much Cat means to him. Cat, was awesome in this one when it came to fighting. I was looking forward to those scenes because she was quite the badass. I really enjoyed the jealousy Cat and Bones felt when it came to their exes. But it did sometimes become too much when all I really wanted was more moments of Bones and Cat together.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1390264465i/8179219._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“You called her Kitten? And she let you? She put me in a coma for three days when I called her that! My balls never recovered from her smashing then into my spine!"<br><br>"And well she should have," Bones agreed. "She's my Kitten, and no one else's” <br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote>Bones was still his sexy, swoony, possessive self. If anything, this book made me love him more. He was Amazing!! I think Bones really does make the series for me, that's how much I love this beautiful vampire. When Bones and Cat reunited, I wasn't sure how they would both react. But I was oh, so happy that the sexual tension between them was very much there. Like I mentioned before, I kept hearing about the infamous Chapter 32. When I finally got to it, Sweet Baby Jesus!! That scene was really HOT!! I didn't know Bones could do those things, and I thoroughly enjoyed it. YOWZA!! He is just the best!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>“I’ll never look at your fangs the same way after last night. A part of me wants to apologize for holding you back before, and the other part wants you to apologize to me because you knew better!” <br><br>He laughed again. "I still have more to show you, trust me..."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</b>
</blockquote>I really enjoyed the this one. I liked the storyline, but for some weird reason, I felt like I liked the first one more. I don't know why exactly. I'm not sure if it was because there weren't as many scenes with Bones and Cat just talking with one another about them together. Maybe it was because I could feel their connection more in the first one than in this one. I can't really tell you what exactly it was. But, I still thought this was a really good second book. I loved it and the ending was crazy!! Seriously loved the ending! I will say one thing, though, I missed my adorkable Timmie from the first one, Ha! Overall, I freaking enjoyed this one, <i>*cough* especially Chapter 32 *cough*</i> and I'm so excited to find out what will happen next. I totally recommend this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="405" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5863584143660470224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_518250630" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/518250630" />
    <a title="Brenna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna"><img alt="Brenna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580475762p2/12928663.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/518250630?book_show_action=true">Jan 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenna" href="/user/show/12928663-brenna">Brenna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/8129187-one-foot-in-the-grave">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=reread">reread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=audible">audible</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/12928663-brenna?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer518250630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15417233886220912199"><b>
  <i>CAUTION! This (audio)book may lead to poor decision making, hazardous driving, and collisions between cars & trashcans.</i>
</b> <br/><br/>Yep, this book is <b>
  <i>that</i>
</b> good! I still maintain that the trashcan came out of nowhere... ;) <br/><br/><i>One Foot in the Grave</i> begins four years after book #1, <i>Halfway to the Grave</i> ends. Cat is working for a secret part of the government being a badass ass, killing vampires everyday, you know, the ushe... Things are pretty rocky with Bones & the story begins with us not knowing how/wh</span>
  <span id="freeText15417233886220912199" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>CAUTION! This (audio)book may lead to poor decision making, hazardous driving, and collisions between cars &amp; trashcans.</i>
</b> <br /><br />Yep, this book is <b>
  <i>that</i>
</b> good! I still maintain that the trashcan came out of nowhere... ;) <br /><br /><i>One Foot in the Grave</i> begins four years after book #1, <i>Halfway to the Grave</i> ends. Cat is working for a secret part of the government being a badass ass, killing vampires everyday, you know, the ushe... Things are pretty rocky with Bones &amp; the story begins with us not knowing how/when we'll get more of our favorite undead hunk. Of course he isn't out of the picture for long, thank goodness! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Careful, luv. I might be angry with you, but that doesn’t mean I don’t still want you. So if you do that again, I’ll shag you right here, right now, and sod anyone who wants to watch.”</i>
</b> SQUEEEE! <br /><br />Cat is in danger, there's a price on her head and everyone wants the infamous "Red Reaper" dead. With the help of Bones, her team (kinda loving Juan &amp; Tate!), and some other random human/undead friends they hatch a plan. Along the way, there are some bumps. Bones has a past and a long list of woman come along with that. It was pretty entertaining to see Cat &amp; Bones's possessiveness. Cat can definitely put an undead ex in their place when needed! Heheheh! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I straddled her, holding the knife still. “I didn’t miss, bitch. One flick of my wrist and you’re a bad memory and an even worse smell. I think we need to have a little talk, woman to skank. I know why you’re doing this. You want me to leave him again, but I can save you the oxygen in your words, because it won’t happen. Bones forgave me for deserting him and running off for years, so you can bet your overused, group-orgy twat that I will forgive him for one bad mouthful of you. Now, are we very clear on that?” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Cat's mom was a pain, like always. Even though I love how Bones gets under her skin, I really hope she ends up coming around at some point. It drives me crazy the way she talks about vampires, when her own daughter is 1/2 vampire. <br /><br />I loved Bones just as much in this one, but Cat not quite as much. She is still really entertaining and funny, but she is much harder and more serious. She's always been really brave and tough, but doesn't have the slight innocence that she had in the first book that I found endearing. <br /><br />And OMG! I experienced the famous <b>CHAPTER 32</b>! Dun dun dun! LOL! It was pretty effing EPIC! HOT HOT HOT! <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’ll never look at your fangs the same way after last night. A part of me wants to apologize for holding you back before, and the other part wants you to apologize to me because you knew better!” </i>
</b><br /><br />I loved this book! I thought the first was slightly better, I can't really put my finger on <i>why</i>, maybe it was just the feeling I had at the end of book 1, I felt like I HAD TO start the next <i>immediately</i>. This one was still amazing and there is a pretty big surprise (make that two) at the end that I definitely wasn't expecting. I'm curious to see where things will go. I love when I feel like I have no clue what's up next in a series! <br /><br /><b><i>“This isn’t going to be easy,” I grumbled as we headed toward the exit. Bones shrugged. “Nothing worthwhile ever is.”</i><br /><br />4.5 stars</b><br /><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_63629985" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Tammy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/785960-tammy"><img alt="Tammy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553824694p2/785960.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/785960-tammy?shelf=humor">humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/785960-tammy?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer63629985" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6383648334325925841">Cat & Bones, Part II packs a punch and leaves you craving more. <br/><br/>The plot moves smoothly, the writing is sharper and wittier than the first book, there is oodles of action, the love scenes left me shaking. Literally. The author writes a particular love scene that is very original and hotter than Hades. <i>I've never read anything like it before!</i><br/><br/>Kudos to Jeaniene Frost for taking a chance and starting this book four years later. Most books in a sequel take place one right on top of the other, but thi</span>
  <span id="freeText6383648334325925841" style="display:none">Cat &amp; Bones, Part II packs a punch and leaves you craving more. <br /><br />The plot moves smoothly, the writing is sharper and wittier than the first book, there is oodles of action, the love scenes left me shaking. Literally. The author writes a particular love scene that is very original and hotter than Hades. <i>I've never read anything like it before!</i><br /><br />Kudos to Jeaniene Frost for taking a chance and starting this book four years later. Most books in a sequel take place one right on top of the other, but this worked for me. Mostly in part because Cat has spent the last four years as a federal agent, training her own speciailized team of vampire killers for a little known branch of Homeland Security. I was thankful I wasn't forced to read all the boring details. Don't get me wrong - the guys on Cat's team are funny, interesting characters who I hope to read about again in the near future. They prove their loyalty to Cat over and over again. But I read these books for one reason and one reason only: Bones. Any page with Bones on it is a <u>Very Good Page</u>. <br /><br />Cat has also spent the past four years trying to adjust to her life without Bones. Unsuccessfully. When attending her best friend's wedding, she runs into an unexpected guest and is reunited with a member of the wedding party. Things heat up almost immediately. Suddenly there are several attemps on Cat's life from both the dead and the undead world. She is forced to trust Bones again as he searches to find the person who placed a hit on his beloved's head. During the process some interesting facts present themself regarding Cat's heritage.<br /> <br />I missed Cat as I met her in the first book - sweeter, funnier with the one-liners, a little more naive'. Now she is bitchier, tougher and drinks and curses more than the first book. I found her jealousy of Bone's former lover, Annette, to be downright funny, but then again it led to the <b>hottest love scene ever</b> so the end justified the means. I just hope that in the next book I can be convinced she deserves the awesomeness that is Bones. If it doesn't work out, then as Gena Showalter so wisely said, "Marry me Bones!"<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6383648334325925841" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_65152493" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/65152493" />
    <a title="Mel" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2295424-mel"><img alt="Mel" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1305638929p2/2295424.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/65152493?book_show_action=true">Jul 27, 2009</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mel" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mel" href="/user/show/2295424-mel">Mel</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer65152493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2085111485113703132">What’s up with the attitude Cat? <br/><br/>I was really disappointed in this second book in the Night Huntress series. <br/>The first book was wonderful. Witty dialogue, a lot of tough action and of course: Cat and Bones together (hot hot hot). We saw Cat being transformed from a shy but determined amateur to a sexy vixen vampire huntress. I loved Bones, I loved Cat and I loved them together.<br/><br/>Four years later, Cat is in charge of a special task force dealing with undead felons. She has a busy work life, her col</span>
  <span id="freeText2085111485113703132" style="display:none">What’s up with the attitude Cat? <br /><br />I was really disappointed in this second book in the Night Huntress series. <br />The first book was wonderful. Witty dialogue, a lot of tough action and of course: Cat and Bones together (hot hot hot). We saw Cat being transformed from a shy but determined amateur to a sexy vixen vampire huntress. I loved Bones, I loved Cat and I loved them together.<br /><br />Four years later, Cat is in charge of a special task force dealing with undead felons. She has a busy work life, her colleagues respect her and love her and she loves them back. Her private life, though, is empty. She misses Bones, feels lonely and is bitter. Very bitter. Very, <i>very</i> bitter. <br />In fact, Cat seems to be doing nothing else than drink, bark at foe AND friend and curse non stop. Now I really don’t mind a tough heroine with a foul mouth but Cat is downright a bitch. Her team of guys respect her and will do anything for her and still she’s sulking and barking!<br /><br />And I hate that. I hate it when I can’t sympathize with the protagonist. Suddenly it’s not so great seeing Cat and Bones together as I clearly felt she did not deserve him. I’m glad Cat pointed that out herself somewhere in the book. <br /><br />Besides the fact that I had trouble liking Cat, I also had trouble with the plot. There were so many good ideas but I didn't think they were worked out well. The party at Ian, Cat meeting her dad, Cat versus Tate, all things that -to me- needed more build up and tension. <br />I have trouble accepting some of the solutions Frost brought up for the problems. I don’t want to spoil anything but let’s just say it was just too fast too easy. <br /><br />The last 10 pages of the book were a prime example of it. This made it feel a little Disney-ish to me, but it did show a sensitive side of Cat I really needed to see again. <br /><br />To me this saved the book. This and Bones of course. Every page with him in it is a pleasure to read. How can you not love the guy?<br />Thanks to Bones, this books earns 2,5 stars. I'll be reading the third installment next and hope I'll like Cat better this time. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2085111485113703132" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1425983742" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1425983742" />
    <a title="Gavin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin"><img alt="Gavin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1338207884p2/8192509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1425983742?book_show_action=true">Oct 26, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Gavin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Gavin" href="/user/show/8192509-gavin">Gavin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8192509-gavin?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1425983742" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13146709849563639739">This was a fun second instalment in the <i>Night Huntress</i> series. It was not quite as good as <i>Halfway to the Grave</i>, but I blame the lacklustre secondary characters for that rather than Cat and Bones. <br/><br/>I was initially a bit horrified that Jeaniene Frost had chosen to kick this book off 4 years after the events at the end of the first book. I usually hate such time jumps, but in this case I think it actually worked out for the best. Cat had a chance to grow on her own and perfect her vampire slaying s</span>
  <span id="freeText13146709849563639739" style="display:none">This was a fun second instalment in the <i>Night Huntress</i> series. It was not quite as good as <i>Halfway to the Grave</i>, but I blame the lacklustre secondary characters for that rather than Cat and Bones. <br /><br />I was initially a bit horrified that Jeaniene Frost had chosen to kick this book off 4 years after the events at the end of the first book. I usually hate such time jumps, but in this case I think it actually worked out for the best. Cat had a chance to grow on her own and perfect her vampire slaying skills. She also got the chance to settle into her role as leader of a secret government vampire slaying squad. Best of all we did not have to suffer through her years separated from Bones! <br /><br />I'm still enjoying the mix of action, humor, and romance that this series has to offer.<br /><br />Rating: 4 stars.<br /><br />Audio Note: Tavia Gilbert did a great job with the audio. I've even gotten used to her voice for Bones.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13146709849563639739" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5297890968755778990">One Foot In The Grave is the second installment of Night Huntress series and it is better than the first one. Bones is pretty different from the man he used to be in the previous book, more adorable and attractive, and yes, he's head over heels in love with Cat! (Why her!? I still don't get that!) Cat, on the other hand, is still that same annoying woman whom I can't bring myself to like. <br/><br/>However, the story had a lot of interesting details, engaging plot, and it was fast-paced enough to hold my </span>
  <span id="freeText5297890968755778990" style="display:none">One Foot In The Grave is the second installment of Night Huntress series and it is better than the first one. Bones is pretty different from the man he used to be in the previous book, more adorable and attractive, and yes, he's head over heels in love with Cat! (Why her!? I still don't get that!) Cat, on the other hand, is still that same annoying woman whom I can't bring myself to like. <br /><br />However, the story had a lot of interesting details, engaging plot, and it was fast-paced enough to hold my attention throughout. Besides, I really did enjoy reading this book so I sure will continue this series.</span>

<div id="review_136218324" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/136218324" />
    <a title="Sarah Mac" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4490376-sarah-mac"><img alt="Sarah Mac" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499925811p2/4490376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/136218324?book_show_action=true">Dec 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah Mac" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah Mac" href="/user/show/4490376-sarah-mac">Sarah Mac</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=read-regifted">read-regifted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=uber-disappointing">uber-disappointing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=zzz-2012">zzz-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=mary-sue-puke-bucket">mary-sue-puke-bucket</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=zzz-2012-leftovers-completed">zzz-2012-leftovers-completed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=drank-the-haterade">drank-the-haterade</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4490376-sarah-mac?shelf=zzz-departed-uf-pnr-junkfood">zzz-departed-uf-pnr-junkfood</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer136218324" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10616857830385942333">It's been a long time since I read the first book in this series (<i>Halfway to the Grave</i>), but I remember enjoying it quite a bit. Half-vamp heritage aside, Cat was an average Ohio girl. She wanted to be badass, but didn't know how to manage it -- so while Bones taught her to kill & embrace her strengths, they fell in love. It felt natural. It made me smile.<br/><br/>This book didn't make me smile. This book made me want to kick Cat in the face.<br/><br/>I should mention that I'm biased against Mega-Alpha Females in </span>
  <span id="freeText10616857830385942333" style="display:none">It's been a long time since I read the first book in this series (<i>Halfway to the Grave</i>), but I remember enjoying it quite a bit. Half-vamp heritage aside, Cat was an average Ohio girl. She wanted to be badass, but didn't know how to manage it -- so while Bones taught her to kill &amp; embrace her strengths, they fell in love. It felt natural. It made me smile.<br /><br />This book didn't make me smile. This book made me want to kick Cat in the face.<br /><br />I should mention that I'm biased against Mega-Alpha Females in paranormal books. I really hate when authors use a foul mouth &amp; asskicking as the embodiments of feminine strength. There's got to be more. A heroine can make mistakes. She can get her ass handed to her. She can pick herself up without lashing out at her boss, her teammates, &amp; anyone with a kind word. <i>Just because she's backed into a corner doesn't mean she's got to screech &amp; claw.</i> Showing delicate emotions outside her interaction with the love interest doesn't make her weak. <br /><br />But for whatever reason, Ms Frost completely abandoned Cat's vulnerabilities -- the things in <i>Halfway</i> that made her imperfect &amp; different from the usual badass paranormal neo-noir heroine. We don't get to see anything of Cat's growing into her new job. Instead we're tossed headfirst into Cat's uber-perfect badassery FOUR YEARS after the close of Book 1. Apparently she doesn't make mistakes anymore. She's Superman. She's Batman. She's Professor X, Wolverine, Rogue, &amp; Magneto all rolled into one...and she's got a team of ultimate badasses to follow her orders, guard the car, &amp; clean up after her one-woman wrecking crew routine. Lovely. It seems Cat's only weakness is her separation from Bones. When she's not beating people senseless or drinking gin from the bottle, she's mooning over Bones -- or rather, her lack thereof. But one day, a mysteriously appearing Best Girlfriend invites him to a wedding. Oh noes! Romance returns to her empty love life! <br /><br />Of course there are fight scenes sprinkled throughout, but they felt unconnected -- token violence to earn the Paranormal label. There's also something vaguely sinister in the background, a plot that revolves around a mystery person contracting hits on Cat's life. Oh, wait...they already know who's behind it, thanks to Bones doing all the work off-screen. Then there's the mystery about Cat's familial relationship with her boss. Oh, wait...they hash that out in one long conversation, thanks to Bones' informants. Then there's the sad sobbing mess of trodden-upon Tate, Cat's second in command who's desperately in love with her. Oh, wait...both Cat &amp; Bones explain repeatedly that she'll never be with Tate, so tough luck. Then there's the tension about Bones' many previous lovers. Oh, wait...Cat fights with one &amp; earns grudging respect (of course), bookended by infodump conversations that are supposed to build character but instead offer brief respites between Cat's wanting to jump Bones. Then there's Sarah clutching her head &amp; wishing for any sort of sustained tension in this novel that isn't solved by Excedrin &amp; chocolate. Oh, wait...<br /><br />:P<br /><br />Seriously, the plot of this novel is loose &amp; lacking. Everything is solved without a hitch. All the plans come to fruition as they should; all the necessary emotional steps are mounted after one (or more) soul-bearing conversations that would make Jung proud. It's much more of a romance than an action story -- Cat &amp; Bones have lots of sex, &amp; not all of it fades to black. While I thought their love scenes in Book 1 were sexy &amp; sweet, these were just...bland. It's one mind-blowing orgasm after another, &amp; the dreaded Buttsex chapter was trying too hard to be kinky while wrapped in a vanilla-romance.<br /><br />In summary: you know a book is irksome when the cliched Latino sidekick's predictible innuendo serves as your sanity yardstick.<br /><br />This had been on my TBR for years, but now it's going in my Paperback Swap box. What a disappointment. :( I still like Bones (even with his unfortunate Austin Powers brit-speak) &amp; Spade (wish he'd had more than three speaking lines), so I'll plow through #3. But my hopes are effectively dashed. If I hadn't bought #3 when I bought #2, I wouldn't be bothering. Sigh.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10616857830385942333" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('YUDj+nL9xj7NLd0MAi55Z6tYTCqgHs+0UkJQUzgFRK+0pPJFQKobtbXk4KKOsZVwzgQ+BB8tgU5oUNVZgQ8c5A==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {

  }

<span id="freeTextContainer2776747891677480229">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on </span>
  <span id="freeText2776747891677480229" style="display:none">Jeaniene Frost is the New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author of the Night Huntress series, the Night Prince series, the Broken Destiny series, and the new Night Rebel series. To date, foreign rights for her novels have sold to twenty different countries. Jeaniene lives in Florida with her husband Matthew, who long ago accepted that she rarely cooks and always sleeps in on the weekends. Aside from writing, Jeaniene enjoys reading, poetry, watching movies with her husband, exploring old cemeteries, spelunking and traveling – by car. Airplanes, children, and cook books frighten her.<br /><br />For information on Jeaniene's books, book trailers, deleted scenes, creature mythology, and more, please visit: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jeanienefrost.com">www.jeanienefrost.com</a><br /></span>
